</div></div></div><div class="ppcmsnodeweb-tmvyzy"><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row1" aria-controls="accordion-content1" aria-expanded="true" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-What is the cost of PayPal platform solutions?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;smb_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">What is the cost of PayPal platform solutions?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content1" aria-labelledby="accordion-row1" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Platform transaction rates and fees are negotiable across any of our integration models. Contact Sales to discuss the right pricing for your business.</p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row2" aria-controls="accordion-content2" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-Where can I review technical documentation?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;smb_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">Where can I review technical documentation?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content2" aria-labelledby="accordion-row2" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body"><span>Technical documentation for our PayPal Hosted integration can be reviewed in our </span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/multiparty/" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-developer docs&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;smb_text_link_clicked&quot;}">developer docs</a><span>. </div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row3" aria-controls="accordion-content3" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-What support does PayPal offer platforms?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;smb_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">What support does PayPal offer platforms?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content3" aria-labelledby="accordion-row3" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body"><span>Partnering with PayPal opens the door to accelerated growth, optimized revenue, enhanced customer experiences, and access to new business opportunities. Our </span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/us/enterprise/become-a-partner" target="_self" rel="" class="html-text-renderer-link" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;Accordion-Link-Paragraph-PayPal Partners Program&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;smb_text_link_clicked&quot;}">PayPal Partners Program</a><span> offers:</span></p>
<ul><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Onboarding and integration specialists as well as ongoing support</li><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Comprehensive technical documentation, access to APIs, SDKs, and sandbox testing</li><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Technical training and education sessions led by PayPal training experts</li><li class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">Co-marketing opportunities with PayPal and access to a robust library of marketing toolkits with customizable marketing assets</li></ul>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row4" aria-controls="accordion-content4" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-Are there any startup or monthly fees?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;smb_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">Are there any startup or monthly fees?</span>
</span><span class="accordion-item-icon accordion-item-icon-theme-white"><span class="ppcmsnodeweb-1bk0n6-svg-size_md" data-ppui-info="icons_8.24.1__7.46.3" aria-hidden="true" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path d="M13 5a1 1 0 1 0-2 0v6H5a1 1 0 1 0 0 2h6v6a1 1 0 1 0 2 0v-6h6a1 1 0 1 0 0-2h-6V5z" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span></span></span></button></h3><div id="accordion-content4" aria-labelledby="accordion-row4" role="region" style="height:0px;opacity:0;display:none"><p class="body-text-style body-text-size-body">There are no upfront or monthly fees associated with our Platform integrations.</p>
</div></div><div class="accordion-item"><h3 class="accordion-item-heading"><button type="button" class="accordion-item-headline" id="accordion-row5" aria-controls="accordion-content5" aria-expanded="false" data-pa-click="{&quot;link&quot;:&quot;accordionItemHeader-Primary-Does the platform integration have mobile compatibility?&quot;,&quot;event_name&quot;:&quot;smb_button_cta_clicked&quot;}"><span class="accordion-item-headline-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text-container"><span class="accordion-item-headline-text heading-text-style heading-text-size-title">Does the platform integration have mobile compatibility?</span>
